            </select>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group g2-full"><label class="form-label">External Registration Link (Optional)</label><input class="form-input" id="eExtLink" placeholder="e.g. https://unstop.com/..."/></div>
          <div class="form-group g2-full"><label class="form-label">Special Guests (Comma separated names)</label><textarea class="form-input" id="eGuests" rows="2" placeholder="e.g. Dr. Satya Nadella, Mr. Sundar Pichai"></textarea></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Venue *</label><input class="form-input" id="eVenue" placeholder="e.g. Main Auditorium"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Date *</label><input class="form-input" type="date" id="eDate"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Time *</label><input class="form-input" type="time" id="eTime"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Registration Deadline *</label><input class="form-input" type="date" id="eDeadline"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Max Participants</label><input class="form-input" type="number" id="eMax" placeholder="e.g. 100" value="100"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Participation Fee (₹)</label><input class="form-input" type="number" id="eFee" value="0" placeholder="0 = Free"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Payment Receiver UPI / Phone (Req if Fee > 0)</label><input class="form-input" id="eUpi" placeholder="e.g. 9876543210@ybl"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Event Coordinator Name *</label><input class="form-input" id="eCoordName" placeholder="e.g. Rahul Sharma"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Coordinator Contact *</label><input class="form-input" id="eCoordPhone" placeholder="e.g. 9876543210"/></div>
          <div class="form-group g2-full" style="display:flex;gap:.8rem;margin-top:.5rem">
            <button class="btn btn-lg btn-primary" id="postBtn" onclick="postEvent()">🚀 Post Event</button>
            <button class="btn btn-lg btn-ghost" onclick="go('events')">Cancel</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }

  async function postEvent() {
    const title=document.getElementById('eTitle').value.trim();
    const description=document.getElementById('eDesc').value.trim();
    const category=document.getElementById('eCat').value;
    const venue=document.getElementById('eVenue').value.trim();
    const date=document.getElementById('eDate').value;
    const time=document.getElementById('eTime').value;
    const registrationDeadline=document.getElementById('eDeadline').value;
    const externalLink=document.getElementById('eExtLink').value.trim();
    const guests=document.getElementById('eGuests').value.trim();
    const coordinatorName=document.getElementById('eCoordName').value.trim();
    const coordinatorPhone=document.getElementById('eCoordPhone').value.trim();

    if (!title||!description||!category||!venue||!date||!time||!registrationDeadline||!coordinatorName||!coordinatorPhone) { toast('Fill all required fields including coordinator info','error'); return; }
    const btn=document.getElementById('postBtn'); btn.textContent='Posting…'; btn.disabled=true;
    
    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('title', title);
    formData.append('description', description);
    formData.append('category', category);
    formData.append('venue', venue);
    formData.append('date', date);
    formData.append('time', time);
    formData.append('registrationDeadline', registrationDeadline);
    formData.append('maxParticipants', +document.getElementById('eMax').value||100);
    formData.append('participationFee', +document.getElementById('eFee').value||0);
    formData.append('externalLink', externalLink);
    formData.append('paymentUpi', document.getElementById('eUpi')?.value||'');
    formData.append('guests', guests);
    formData.append('coordinatorName', coordinatorName);
    formData.append('coordinatorPhone', coordinatorPhone);

    try {
      await API.createEvent(formData);
      toast('🎉 Event posted!','success');
      await loadClubData();
      setTimeout(()=>go('events'),700);
    } catch (err) { toast(err.message,'error'); btn.textContent='🚀 Post Event'; btn.disabled=false; }
  }

  function renderParticipants() {
    const allPars = myEvents.flatMap(ev=>(ev.registeredStudents||[]).map(s=>{
      const proof = (ev.paymentProofs || []).find(p => p.studentId === s._id || p.studentId?._id === s._id);
      return {
        ...s,
        eventTitle:ev.title,
        proofURL: proof?.proofURL,
        didAttend: (ev.attendedStudents||[]).includes(s._id)
      };
    }));
    document.getElementById('dashMain').innerHTML = `
      <div class="dash-header" style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-end">
        <div><h1>Participants</h1><p>${allPars.length} total registrations across your events</p></div>
        <button class="btn btn-sm btn-success" onclick="exportClubCSV()">⬇️ Export CSV</button>
      </div>
      <div class="section-box">
        ${allPars.map(p=>`<div class="par-row">
          <div class="avatar av-md">${(p.name||'?')[0].toUpperCase()}</div>
          <div style="flex:1">
            <div style="font-size:.88rem;font-weight:600">${p.name||'Student'} <span style="font-weight:400;color:var(--tx2);margin-left:.3rem">(${p.rollNo||'No Roll No'})</span></div>
            <div style="font-size:.74rem;color:var(--tx2)">${p.email||''} · ${p.department||'Unknown Dept'}</div>
            ${p.proofURL ? `<a href="${p.proofURL}" target="_blank" style="font-size:.7rem;color:var(--v);text-decoration:none;font-weight:600;margin-top:.3rem;display:inline-block">🖼️ View Payment Screenshot</a>` : ''}
          </div>
          <div style="text-align:right"><div style="font-size:.8rem;font-weight:500">${p.eventTitle}</div></div>
          <span class="tag ${p.didAttend ? 'tag-gn' : 'tag-am'}" style="margin-left:1rem">${p.didAttend ? '✅ Attended' : '⏳ Registered'}</span>
        </div>`).join('')}
        ${!allPars.length?'<p style="color:var(--tx2)">No registrations yet.</p>':''}
      </div>`;
  }

  function renderScanner() {
    document.getElementById('dashMain').innerHTML = `
      <div class="dash-header"><h1>Scan Tickets 📷</h1><p>Hold the student's QR code up to the camera to instantly check them in.</p></div>
      <div class="section-box" style="text-align:center">
        <div id="reader" style="width:100%;max-width:500px;margin:1rem auto;border-radius:12px;overflow:hidden;border:1px solid var(--b2);background:#fff"></div>
      </div>`;
    
    // Slight delay to ensure DOM is ready before injecting scanner
    setTimeout(() => {
      html5QrcodeScanner = new Html5QrcodeScanner("reader", { fps: 10, qrbox: {width: 250, height: 250} }, false);
      html5QrcodeScanner.render(onScanSuccess, onScanFailure);
    }, 100);
  }

  window.isScanning = false;
  async function onScanSuccess(decodedText, decodedResult) {
    if (window.isScanning) return; // Debounce
    window.isScanning = true;
    try {
      const payload = JSON.parse(decodedText);
      if (!payload.eventId || !payload.studentId) throw new Error("Invalid Format");
      
      if (html5QrcodeScanner) html5QrcodeScanner.pause(true); // Pause scanning
      
      const res = await api('POST', '/events/' + payload.eventId + '/attendance', { studentId: payload.studentId }, true);
      toast(res.message || '✅ Student Checked In!', 'success');
      
      setTimeout(() => { if (html5QrcodeScanner) html5QrcodeScanner.resume(); window.isScanning = false; }, 3000);
    } catch (err) {
      toast(err.message || 'Error processing ticket! Invalid QR?', 'error');
      setTimeout(() => { window.isScanning = false; }, 2000);
    }
  }

  function onScanFailure(error) {
    // Ignore routine frame read failures
  }

  window.exportClubCSV = function() {
    const allPars = myEvents.flatMap(ev=>(ev.registeredStudents||[]).map(s=>({
      ...s, eventTitle:ev.title, didAttend: (ev.attendedStudents||[]).includes(s._id)
    })));
    if (!allPars.length) return toast('No data to export', 'error');
    const csvRows = allPars.map(p => '"' + p.eventTitle + '","' + (p.rollNo||'N/A') + '","' + (p.name||'') + '","' + (p.department||'N/A') + '","' + (p.email||'') + '","' + (p.didAttend?'Attended':'Registered') + '"');
    const csv = "Event,RollNo,Name,Department,Email,Status\\n" + csvRows.join('\\n');
    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url; a.download = 'all_participants.csv';
    a.click();
  };

  async function renderClubProfile() {
    const el=document.getElementById('dashMain');
    if (!myClub) {
      el.innerHTML=`<div class="dash-header"><h1>Club Profile</h1></div>
        <div class="section-box">
          <p style="color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:1.5rem">Register your club to get started.</p>
          <div class="g2">
            <div class="form-group g2-full"><label class="form-label">Club Name *</label><input class="form-input" id="cName" placeholder="e.g. Coding Club"/></div>
            <div class="form-group g2-full"><label class="form-label">Description *</label><textarea class="form-input" id="cDesc" rows="3"></textarea></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Category *</label>
              <select class="form-select" id="cCat"><option value="">Select…</option><option>Technical</option><option>Cultural</option><option>Sports</option><option>Hackathons</option><option>Entrepreneurship</option><option>Arts</option></select>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Contact Email *</label><input class="form-input" id="cEmail" placeholder="e.g. club@college.edu"/></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Contact Phone *</label><input class="form-input" id="cPhone" placeholder="e.g. 9876543210"/></div>
            <div class="form-group g2-full"><button class="btn btn-lg btn-primary" id="cBtn" onclick="createClub()">Register Club</button></div>
          </div>
        </div>`;
      return;
    }
    el.innerHTML=`
      <div class="dash-header"><h1>Club Profile</h1></div>
      <div class="section-box">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:1.4rem;padding-bottom:1.8rem;margin-bottom:1.8rem;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1)">
          <div style="width:68px;height:68px;border-radius:18px;background:rgba(124,107,255,.15);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:2rem">🏢</div>
          <div><h2 style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:1.25rem;font-weight:800">${myClub.clubName}</h2><p style="color:var(--tx2)">${myClub.category}</p>
          <span class="tag ${myClub.isApproved?'tag-gn':'tag-am'}" style="margin-top:.4rem;display:inline-flex">${myClub.isApproved?'✅ Approved':'⏳ Pending Approval'}</span></div>
        </div>
        <div class="g2">
          <div class="form-group g2-full"><label class="form-label">Club Name</label><input class="form-input" id="upName" value="${myClub.clubName}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group g2-full"><label class="form-label">Description</label><textarea class="form-input" id="upDesc" rows="3">${myClub.description}</textarea></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Contact Email</label><input class="form-input" id="upEmail" value="${myClub.contactEmail||''}" placeholder="club@college.edu"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Contact Phone</label><input class="form-input" id="upPhone" value="${myClub.contactPhone||''}" placeholder="9876543210"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Instagram</label><input class="form-input" id="upIG" value="${myClub.socialLinks?.instagram||''}" placeholder="@yourclub"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Website</label><input class="form-input" id="upWeb" value="${myClub.socialLinks?.website||''}" placeholder="https://…"/></div>
          
          <div class="form-group g2-full"><label class="form-label">Gallery Images (Comma separated URLs)</label>
            <textarea class="form-input" id="upGallery" rows="2" placeholder="https://img1.jpg, https://img2.jpg">${(myClub.gallery || []).join(', ')}</textarea>
            <p style="font-size:0.75rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-top:0.3rem">Add links to your past event photos. Comma separated.</p>
          </div>

          <div class="form-group g2-full"><button class="btn btn-md btn-primary" onclick="updateClub()">Save Changes</button></div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }

  async function createClub() {
    const clubName=document.getElementById('cName').value.trim();
    const description=document.getElementById('cDesc').value.trim();
    const category=document.getElementById('cCat').value;
    const contactEmail=document.getElementById('cEmail').value.trim();
    const contactPhone=document.getElementById('cPhone').value.trim();
    if (!clubName||!description||!category||!contactEmail||!contactPhone) { toast('Fill all required fields','error'); return; }
    const btn=document.getElementById('cBtn'); btn.textContent='Registering…'; btn.disabled=true;
    try {
      await API.createClub({ clubName, description, category, contactEmail, contactPhone });
      toast('Club registered! Awaiting admin approval.','success');
      await loadClubData(); buildSidebar(); go('overview');
    } catch (err) { toast(err.message,'error'); btn.textContent='Register Club'; btn.disabled=false; }
  }

  async function updateClub() {
    const clubName=document.getElementById('upName').value.trim();
    const description=document.getElementById('upDesc').value.trim();
    const contactEmail=document.getElementById('upEmail').value.trim();
    const contactPhone=document.getElementById('upPhone').value.trim();
    const instagram=document.getElementById('upIG').value.trim();
    const website=document.getElementById('upWeb').value.trim();
    const galleryRaw=document.getElementById('upGallery').value.trim();
    const gallery = galleryRaw ? galleryRaw.split(',').map(s=>s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];
    try {
      await API.updateClub(myClub._id, { clubName, description, contactEmail, contactPhone, socialLinks:{ instagram, website }, gallery });
      toast('Club updated!','success');
      await loadClubData();
    } catch (err) { toast(err.message,'error'); }
  }

  async function delEvent(id, btn) {
    btn.disabled=true;
    try {
      await API.deleteEvent(id);
      toast('Event deleted','info');
      await loadClubData(); renderMyEvents();
    } catch (err) { toast(err.message,'error'); btn.disabled=false; }
  }

  window.renderEditForm = function(id) {
    const ev = myEvents.find(e => e._id === id);
    if (!ev) return;
    document.getElementById('dashMain').innerHTML = `
      <div class="dash-header"><h1>Edit Event</h1><p>Updating: ${ev.title}</p></div>
      <div class="section-box">
        <div class="g2">
          <div class="form-group g2-full"><label class="form-label">Event Title</label><input class="form-input" id="edTitle" value="${ev.title}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group g2-full"><label class="form-label">Description</label><textarea class="form-input" id="edDesc" rows="3">${ev.description}</textarea></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Venue</label><input class="form-input" id="edVenue" value="${ev.venue}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Date</label><input class="form-input" type="date" id="edDate" value="${ev.date.split('T')[0]}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Time</label><input class="form-input" type="time" id="edTime" value="${ev.time}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Deadline</label><input class="form-input" type="date" id="edDeadline" value="${ev.registrationDeadline.split('T')[0]}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group g2-full"><label class="form-label">Guests (Comma separated)</label><textarea class="form-input" id="edGuests" rows="2">${(ev.guests || []).join(', ')}</textarea></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Fee (₹)</label><input class="form-input" type="number" id="edFee" value="${ev.participationFee}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Max Capacity</label><input class="form-input" type="number" id="edMax" value="${ev.maxParticipants || 100}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Coordinator Name</label><input class="form-input" id="edCoordName" value="${ev.coordinatorName || ''}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Coordinator Contact</label><input class="form-input" id="edCoordPhone" value="${ev.coordinatorPhone || ''}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group g2-full"><button class="btn btn-lg btn-primary" id="saveEditBtn" onclick="saveEditEvent('${ev._id}')">Save Changes</button> <button class="btn btn-lg btn-ghost" onclick="go('events')">Cancel</button></div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }

  window.saveEditEvent = async function(id) {
    const title = document.getElementById('edTitle').value.trim();
    const description = document.getElementById('edDesc').value.trim();
    const venue = document.getElementById('edVenue').value.trim();
    const date = document.getElementById('edDate').value;
    const time = document.getElementById('edTime').value;
    const registrationDeadline = document.getElementById('edDeadline').value;
    const participationFee = +document.getElementById('edFee').value;
    const maxParticipants = +document.getElementById('edMax').value;
    const guests = document.getElementById('edGuests').value.trim();
    const coordinatorName = document.getElementById('edCoordName').value.trim();
    const coordinatorPhone = document.getElementById('edCoordPhone').value.trim();

    const btn = document.getElementById('saveEditBtn');
    btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = 'Updating...';

    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('title', title);
    formData.append('description', description);
    formData.append('venue', venue);
    formData.append('date', date);
    formData.append('time', time);
    formData.append('registrationDeadline', registrationDeadline);
    formData.append('participationFee', participationFee);
    formData.append('maxParticipants', maxParticipants);
    formData.append('guests', guests);
    formData.append('coordinatorName', coordinatorName);
    formData.append('coordinatorPhone', coordinatorPhone);

    try {
      await API.updateEvent(id, formData);
      toast('Event updated successfully!', 'success');
      await loadClubData(); go('events');
    } catch (err) { toast(err.message, 'error'); btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Save Changes'; }
  }

  window.exportClubCSV = function() {
    const allPars = myEvents.flatMap(ev=>(ev.registeredStudents||[]).map(s=>({
      ...s,
      eventTitle:ev.title
    })));
    if(!allPars.length) return toast('No registrations to export','error');
    
    const csvRows = allPars.map(p => `"${p.rollNo||'N/A'}","${p.name||''}","${p.eventTitle}","${p.department||'N/A'}","${p.phone||'N/A'}","${p.email||''}"`);
    const csv = "RollNo,Name,Event,Department,Phone,Email\n" + csvRows.join('\n');
    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url; a.download = 'campusconnect_registrations.csv';
    a.click();
    toast('List downloaded!', 'success');
  }

  async function init() {
    await loadClubData();
    buildSidebar();
    go('overview');
  }

  init();
</script>
</body>
</html>


// FILE: pages\clubs.html
// ========================================
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en" data-theme="dark">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8"/><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1.0"/>
  <title>Clubs — CampusConnect</title>
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/style.css"/>
  <style>
    .clubs-grid{display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr);gap:1.4rem}
    .club-card{background:var(--s1);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:var(--rl);padding:1.8rem;transition:all .25s;cursor:pointer;position:relative;overflow:hidden}
    .club-card:hover{transform:translateY(-4px);border-color:var(--b2);box-shadow:var(--sh)}
    .cc-head{display:flex;align-items:center;gap:1rem;margin-bottom:1rem}
    .cc-icon{width:50px;height:50px;border-radius:14px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:1.55rem;flex-shrink:0}
    .cc-name{font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:.95rem;font-weight:700}
    .cc-cat{font-size:.75rem;color:var(--tx2)}
    .cc-desc{font-size:.83rem;color:var(--tx2);line-height:1.6;margin-bottom:1rem;display:-webkit-box;-webkit-line-clamp:2;-webkit-box-orient:vertical;overflow:hidden}
    .cc-stats{display:flex;gap:1.2rem;padding-top:.8rem;border-top:1px solid var(--b1)}
    .cc-stat{font-size:.75rem;color:var(--tx2)}
    .cc-stat strong{display:block;font-size:.95rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx);font-family:'Syne',sans-serif}
    @media(max-width:900px){.clubs-grid{grid-template-columns:repeat(2,1fr)}}
    @media(max-width:580px){.clubs-grid{grid-template-columns:1fr}}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
<nav class="navbar" id="mainNav"></nav>
<div class="page-wrap">
  <div class="page-hero" style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(255,107,157,.08),rgba(247,201,72,.04))">
    <div class="container">
      <span class="section-label">✦ Explore</span>
      <h1>All Clubs</h1>
      <p style="color:var(--tx2);margin-top:.4rem">Discover clubs that match your passion and interests.</p>
    </div>
  </div>
  <div class="container" style="padding:2rem 0 4rem">
    <div class="filters">
      <div class="search-box"><span class="s-ico">🔍</span><input type="text" id="searchInput" placeholder="Search clubs…"/></div>
      <div class="cat-pills" id="catPills"></div>
    </div>
    <div id="resultsInfo" style="margin-bottom:1.2rem;color:var(--tx2);font-size:.85rem"></div>
    <div class="clubs-grid" id="clubsGrid"></div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Club Modal -->
<div class="modal-overlay" id="clubModal">
  <div class="modal">
    <div class="modal-header"><div class="modal-title" id="mTitle"></div><button class="modal-close" onclick="closeModal()">✕</button></div>
    <div id="mBody"></div>
  </div>
</div>

<footer id="mainFooter"></footer>
<script src="../js/app.js"></script>
<script>
  buildNav('clubs');

  const CATS = ['All','Technical','Cultural','Sports','Entrepreneurship','Arts','Other'];
  const COLORS = { Technical:'#7c6bff',Cultural:'#ff6b9d',Sports:'#4ade80',Entrepreneurship:'#f7c948',Arts:'#a594ff',Other:'#3de6c0',Hackathons:'#f7c948',Workshops:'#3de6c0' };
  const ICONS = { Technical:'💻',Cultural:'🎭',Sports:'⚽',Entrepreneurship:'🚀',Arts:'🎨',Other:'🏢',Hackathons:'🏆',Workshops:'🔧' };

  let allClubs = [];
  let activeCat = 'All', search = '';

  const pillsEl = document.getElementById('catPills');
  CATS.forEach(c => {
    const b = document.createElement('button');
    b.className='cat-pill'+(c==='All'?' active':''); b.textContent=c;
    b.onclick=()=>{ activeCat=c; document.querySelectorAll('.cat-pill').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('active')); b.classList.add('active'); render(); };
    pillsEl.appendChild(b);
  });

  document.getElementById('searchInput').addEventListener('input', e => { search=e.target.value.toLowerCase(); render(); });

  async function loadClubs() {
    const grid = document.getElementById('clubsGrid');
    loading(grid);
    try {
      allClubs = await API.getClubs();
      render();
    } catch {
      grid.innerHTML = `<div style="grid-column:1/-1;text-align:center;padding:4rem"><p style="color:var(--tx2)">⚠️ Backend not connected. Start your server on port 5000.</p></div>`;
    }
  }

  function render() {
    let list = [...allClubs];
    if (activeCat!=='All') list=list.filter(c=>c.category===activeCat);
    if (search) list=list.filter(c=>c.clubName.toLowerCase().includes(search)||c.description.toLowerCase().includes(search));
    document.getElementById('resultsInfo').textContent = `${list.length} club${list.length!==1?'s':''} found`;
    const grid = document.getElementById('clubsGrid');
    if (!list.length) { empty(grid,'No clubs found.','🏢'); return; }

    grid.innerHTML = list.map(cl => {
      const color = COLORS[cl.category]||'#7c6bff';
      const icon  = ICONS[cl.category]||'🏢';
      return `<div class="club-card" onclick="openModal('${cl._id}')">
        <div style="position:absolute;top:0;left:0;right:0;height:3px;background:${color};border-radius:var(--rl) var(--rl) 0 0"></div>
        <div class="cc-head">
          <div class="cc-icon" style="background:${color}22">${cl.logoURL?`<img src="${cl.logoURL}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;border-radius:14px">`:`${icon}`}</div>
          <div><div class="cc-name">${cl.clubName}</div><div class="cc-cat">${cl.category}</div></div>
        </div>
        <div class="cc-desc">${cl.description}</div>
        <div class="cc-stats">
          <div class="cc-stat"><strong>${cl.events?.length||0}</strong>Events</div>
          <div class="cc-stat"><strong>${new Date(cl.createdAt).getFullYear()}</strong>Founded</div>
          <div class="cc-stat"><strong style="color:var(--gn)">✅</strong>Approved</div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
  }

  async function toggleFollow(id, btn, isFollowing) {
    if (!Auth.isLoggedIn) { window.location.href='login.html'; return; }
    if (Auth.user.role!=='student') { toast('Only students can follow clubs','error'); return; }
    btn.disabled = true;
    try {
      if (isFollowing) {
        await API.unfollowClub(id);
        toast('Unfollowed club', 'info');
        const u = Auth.user; u.followingClubs = u.followingClubs.filter(c => c !== id); Auth.save(u, Auth.token);
      } else {
        await API.followClub(id);
        toast('Followed club!', 'success');
        const u = Auth.user; u.followingClubs = u.followingClubs || []; u.followingClubs.push(id); Auth.save(u, Auth.token);
      }
      closeModal();
      openModal(id);
    } catch(err) {
      toast(err.message, 'error');
      btn.disabled = false;
    }
  }

  async function openModal(id) {
    try {
      const cl = await API.getClub(id);
      const color = COLORS[cl.category]||'#7c6bff';
      const icon  = ICONS[cl.category]||'🏢';
      
      let followBtnHtml = '';
      if (Auth.user?.role === 'student') {
          const isFollowing = (Auth.user.followingClubs || []).includes(cl._id);
          followBtnHtml = `<button class="btn btn-sm ${isFollowing?'btn-success':'btn-primary'}" style="margin-top:1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem" onclick="toggleFollow('${cl._id}', this, ${isFollowing})">${isFollowing?'✅ Following':'Follow Club'}</button>`;
      }

      document.getElementById('mTitle').textContent = cl.clubName;
      document.getElementById('mBody').innerHTML = `
        <div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;background:${color}11;border-radius:var(--r);margin-bottom:1.5rem;font-size:3rem">${icon}</div>
        <div style="margin-bottom:1rem;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;">
            ${catTag(cl.category)}
            <div style="font-size:0.8rem;color:var(--tx2)">👥 ${cl.followersCount || 0} followers</div>
        </div>
        ${followBtnHtml}
        <p style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.88rem;line-height:1.7;margin-bottom:1.5rem">${cl.description}</p>

        <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:12px;padding:1.2rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem">
          <h4 style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.8rem;text-transform:uppercase">Contact Organizer</h4>
          <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:.6rem;font-size:.85rem">
            ${cl.contactEmail ? `<div><span style="color:var(--tx2)">📧 Email:</span> <a href="mailto:${cl.contactEmail}" style="color:var(--v);text-decoration:none;font-weight:600">${cl.contactEmail}</a></div>` : ''}
            ${cl.contactPhone ? `<div><span style="color:var(--tx2)">📞 Phone:</span> <span style="font-weight:600">${cl.contactPhone}</span></div>` : ''}
            ${cl.socialLinks?.instagram ? `<div><span style="color:var(--tx2)">📸 Insta:</span> <a href="${cl.socialLinks.instagram}" target="_blank" style="color:var(--v);text-decoration:none;font-weight:600">${cl.socialLinks.instagram.split('/').pop() || 'Profile'}</a></div>` : ''}
          </div>
        </div>

        ${(cl.gallery && cl.gallery.length > 0) ? `
          <h4 style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:.85rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.8rem;letter-spacing:.5px;text-transform:uppercase">GALLERY</h4>
          <div style="display:flex;gap:.5rem;overflow-x:auto;padding-bottom:1rem;margin-bottom:1rem">
            ${cl.gallery.map(url => `<img src="${url}" style="height:100px;border-radius:8px;object-fit:cover;border:1px solid var(--b1)">`).join('')}
          </div>
        ` : ''}

        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(2,1fr);gap:.7rem;margin-bottom:1.4rem">
          <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.8rem;text-align:center">
            <div style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:800;color:${color}">${cl.events?.length||0}</div>
            <div style="font-size:.7rem;color:var(--tx2)">Events</div>
          </div>
          <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.8rem;text-align:center">
            <div style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:800;color:${color}">${new Date(cl.createdAt).getFullYear()}</div>
            <div style="font-size:.7rem;color:var(--tx2)">Founded</div>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${cl.events?.length?`<h4 style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:.85rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.8rem;letter-spacing:.5px;text-transform:uppercase">EVENTS</h4>
        ${cl.events.map(ev=>`<div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.85rem;margin-bottom:.5rem;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center">
          <div style="font-size:.85rem;font-weight:600">${ev.title||ev}</div>
          <span style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--tx2)">${ev.date?fDate(ev.date):''}</span>
        </div>`).join('')}`:''}
        <a href="events.html" class="btn btn-md btn-primary" style="width:100%;margin-top:1rem;display:flex">View All Events →</a>`;
      document.getElementById('clubModal').classList.add('open');
    } catch { toast('Failed to load club details','error'); }
  }

  function closeModal() { document.getElementById('clubModal').classList.remove('open'); }
  document.getElementById('clubModal').addEventListener('click', e=>{if(e.target===e.currentTarget)closeModal();});

  loadClubs();
</script>
</body>
</html>


// FILE: pages\dashboard.html
// ========================================
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en" data-theme="dark">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8"/><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1.0"/>
  <title>Dashboard — CampusConnect</title>
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/style.css"/>
  <style>
    .ev-row{background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.9rem 1.1rem;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:.9rem;margin-bottom:.6rem;transition:all .2s}
    .ev-row:hover{border-color:var(--b2)}
    .ev-ico{width:40px;height:40px;border-radius:10px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:1.2rem;flex-shrink:0;background:rgba(124,107,255,.15)}
    .notif{background:var(--s2);border-left:3px solid var(--v);border-radius:0 10px 10px 0;padding:.85rem 1rem;margin-bottom:.55rem;font-size:.84rem}
    .notif.tl{border-color:var(--tl)}.notif.pk{border-color:var(--pk)}
    .int-chip-sm{display:inline-flex;align-items:center;padding:.25rem .7rem;border-radius:100px;font-size:.72rem;font-weight:600;background:rgba(124,107,255,.15);color:var(--v2);border:1px solid rgba(124,107,255,.25);margin:.15rem}
    .int-chip-sm.sel{background:var(--v);color:#fff;border-color:var(--v2)}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
<nav class="navbar" id="mainNav"></nav>
<div class="page-wrap">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="dash-layout">
      <aside class="sidebar" id="sidebar"></aside>
      <main class="dash-main" id="dashMain"></main>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

  </div>

<script src="../js/app.js?v=2"></script>
<script>
  buildNav('');
  if (!Auth.isLoggedIn) { window.location.href='login.html'; }
  const user = Auth.user;
  if (user?.role==='clubAdmin') { window.location.href='club-dashboard.html'; }
  if (user?.role==='superAdmin') { window.location.href='admin.html'; }

  let page = 'overview';

  function buildSidebar() {
    const links = [
      {k:'overview',i:'🏠',l:'Overview'},
      {k:'events',i:'📅',l:'Upcoming Events'},
      {k:'clubs',i:'🏢',l:'Discover Clubs'},
      {k:'registered',i:'✅',l:'My Registrations'},
      {k:'profile',i:'👤',l:'Profile Settings'},
    ];
    document.getElementById('sidebar').innerHTML = `
      <div class="sidebar-profile">
        <div class="avatar av-lg">${user.name[0].toUpperCase()}</div>
        <h3 style="margin-top:.6rem">${user.name}</h3>
        <p>${user.email}</p>
        <div style="margin-top:.4rem"><span class="tag tag-v">🎓 Student</span></div>
      </div>
      <nav class="sidebar-nav">
        ${links.map(l=>`<button class="s-link${l.k===page?' active':''}" onclick="go('${l.k}')"><span class="ico">${l.i}</span>${l.l}</button>`).join('')}
        <button class="s-link" onclick="Auth.clear()" style="margin-top:1rem;color:var(--rd)"><span class="ico">🚪</span>Logout</button>
      </nav>`;
  }

  async function go(p) {
    page=p; buildSidebar();
    const el = document.getElementById('dashMain');
    loading(el);
    if (p==='overview')   await renderOverview();
    if (p==='events')     await renderEvents();
    if (p==='registered') await renderRegistered();
    if (p==='clubs')      await renderClubs();
    if (p==='profile')    renderProfile();
  }

  async function renderClubs() {
    const el = document.getElementById('dashMain');
    try {
      const clubs = await API.getClubs();
      el.innerHTML = `
        <div class="dash-header"><h1>Discover Clubs</h1><p>Join or follow campus organizations.</p></div>
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fit, minmax(280px, 1fr));gap:1.2rem">
          ${clubs.map(cl => `
            <div class="row" style="padding:1.2rem;flex-direction:column;align-items:flex-start;gap:.6rem;cursor:pointer" onclick="window.location.href='clubs.html'">
              <div style="display:flex;gap:.8rem;align-items:center;width:100%">
                <div style="width:42px;height:42px;border-radius:10px;background:rgba(124,107,255,0.1);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:1.2rem;flex-shrink:0">🏢</div>
                <div style="flex:1"><div style="font-weight:700;font-size:.9rem">${cl.clubName}</div><div style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--tx2)">${cl.category}</div></div>
              </div>
              <p style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--tx2);line-height:1.5;margin-bottom:.5rem">${cl.description.slice(0, 80)}...</p>
              <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;width:100%;align-items:center">
                <span style="font-size:.7rem;color:var(--v2);font-weight:600">📊 ${cl.events?.length || 0} Events</span>
                <span class="tag tag-v" style="font-size:.65rem">View Profile →</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          `).join('')}
        </div>
      `;
    } catch (err) { el.innerHTML = `<p style="color:var(--rd)">${err.message}</p>`; }
  }

  async function renderOverview() {
    const el = document.getElementById('dashMain');
    try {
      const [dashData, upcomingEvs, notifs] = await Promise.all([API.getDashboard(), API.getEvents(), API.getNotifications()]);
      const regCount = dashData.registeredEvents?.length||0;
      const upcoming = upcomingEvs.filter(e=>new Date(e.date).setHours(23,59,59,999)>=Date.now()).slice(0,10);
      el.innerHTML = `
        <div class="dash-header"><h1>Good morning, ${user.name.split(' ')[0]} 👋</h1><p>Here's what's happening on campus.</p></div>
        <div class="stat-grid">
          <div class="stat-card"><div class="ico">✅</div><div class="val">${regCount}</div><div class="lbl">Registered</div></div>
          <div class="stat-card"><div class="ico">📅</div><div class="val">${upcomingEvs.filter(e=>new Date(e.date).setHours(23,59,59,999)>=Date.now()).length}</div><div class="lbl">Upcoming</div></div>
          <div class="stat-card"><div class="ico">🎯</div><div class="val">${user.interests?.length||0}</div><div class="lbl">My Interests</div></div>
          <div class="stat-card"><div class="ico">🏢</div><div class="val">${user.followingClubs?.length||0}</div><div class="lbl">Following</div></div>
        </div>
        <div class="section-box">
          <div class="box-title">🔔 Notifications <button class="btn btn-sm btn-ghost" onclick="markAllRead()" style="font-size:.7rem">Mark all as read</button></div>
          <div id="notifList"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-grid" id="followedFeed" style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr;gap:1.1rem;margin-top:2rem">
           <!-- Followed Clubs Feed will be injected here -->
        </div>
        <div class="section-box">
          <div class="box-title">📅 Upcoming Events <a href="#" onclick="go('events')" style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--v2);font-weight:500">View all →</a></div>
          ${upcoming.map(ev=>`<div class="ev-row">
            <div class="ev-ico">🎯</div>
            <div style="flex:1"><div style="font-size:.88rem;font-weight:600">${ev.title}</div><div style="font-size:.76rem;color:var(--tx2)">📅 ${fDate(ev.date)} · 📍 ${ev.venue} · 🏢 ${ev.clubId?.clubName || 'Club'}</div></div>
            ${catTag(ev.category)}
          </div>`).join('')}
          ${!upcoming.length?'<p style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.85rem">No upcoming events yet.</p>':''}
        </div>`;
      
      // 1. Generate Interest-based Notifications dynamically
      const registeredIds = (dashData.registeredEvents || []).map(e=>e._id||e);
      const myInterests = user.interests || [];
      const interestEvs = upcomingEvs.filter(e => 
          new Date(e.date) >= Date.now() && 
          !registeredIds.includes(e._id) && 
          myInterests.includes(e.category)
      );

      let interestNotifsHTML = '';
      if (interestEvs.length > 0) {
        interestNotifsHTML = interestEvs.slice(0, 2).map(ev => 
          `<div class="notif tl" style="cursor:pointer" onclick="go('events')">
            💡 <strong>Based on your interests:</strong> Check out <strong>${ev.title}</strong> (${ev.category}) on ${fDate(ev.date)}!
          </div>`
        ).join('');
      } else if (myInterests.length === 0) {
        interestNotifsHTML = `<div class="notif pk" style="cursor:pointer" onclick="go('profile')">
          ⚠️ <strong>Update your Profile:</strong> Set your interests in Profile Settings to get personalized event alerts!
        </div>`;
      }

      // 2. Fetch standard notifications
      let baseNotifsHTML = '';
      if (notifs && notifs.length) {
        baseNotifsHTML = notifs.map(n => `<div class="notif ${n.isRead?'':'pk'}" style="cursor:pointer" onclick="markRead('${n._id}', this)">
          <strong>${n.title}</strong>: ${n.message}
          <div style="font-size:0.7rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-top:0.2rem">${fDate(n.createdAt)} ${n.isRead?'':'· <span style="color:var(--pk)">New</span>'}</div>
        </div>`).join('');
      } else {
        baseNotifsHTML = `<div class="notif">📢 Welcome to CampusConnect! Stay tuned for updates.</div>`;
      }
      
      document.getElementById('notifList').innerHTML = interestNotifsHTML + baseNotifsHTML;

      // Inject followed club updates
      renderFollowedFeed();
    } catch (err) {
      el.innerHTML = `<div class="dash-header"><h1>Dashboard</h1></div><div class="section-box"><p style="color:var(--rd)">Failed to load: ${err.message}</p></div>`;
    }
  }

  async function markRead(id, el) {
    try {
      await API.markNotifRead(id);
      el.classList.remove('pk');
      const badge = el.querySelector('span');
      if (badge) badge.remove();
    } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
  }

  async function markAllRead() {
    try {
      await API.markAllNotifsRead();
      document.querySelectorAll('.notif.pk').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('pk'));
      toast('All caught up!', 'info');
      go('overview');
    } catch (e) { toast(e.message, 'error'); }
  }

  async function renderEvents() {
    const el = document.getElementById('dashMain');
    try {
      // Fetch events, dashboard data, and AI recommendations
      const [events, dashData, recommended] = await Promise.all([API.getEvents(), API.getDashboard(), API.getRecommendedEvents()]);
      const registeredIds = (dashData.registeredEvents || []).map(e => e._id || e);
      const upcoming = events.filter(e => new Date(e.date).setHours(23,59,59,999) >= Date.now()).sort((a,b) => new Date(a.date) - new Date(b.date));
      
      const renderCard = (ev, isGlowing = false) => {
        const isReg = registeredIds.includes(ev._id);
        const pct = ev.maxParticipants ? Math.round((ev.registeredStudents.length / ev.maxParticipants) * 100) : 0;
        return `<div class="event-card" style="${isGlowing?'border:2px solid var(--v);box-shadow:0 8px 25px rgba(124,107,255,.15)':''}">
          <div class="ec-img" style="background:var(--s2);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:3.5rem"> 
            ${(() => {
              const icons = { 'Technical': '💻', 'Cultural': '🎭', 'Sports': '🏆', 'Hackathons': '🚀', 'Workshops': '🛠️', 'Entrepreneurship': '💡', 'Arts': '🎨' };
              return icons[ev.category] || '🎯';
            })()}
            <div style="position:absolute;top:.8rem;left:.8rem">${catTag(ev.category)}</div>
            <div style="position:absolute;top:.8rem;right:.8rem"><span class="tag ${ev.participationFee===0?'tag-gn':'tag-am'}">${ev.participationFee===0?'Free':'₹'+ev.participationFee}</span></div>
          </div>
          <div class="ec-body">
            <div class="ec-club">🏢 ${ev.clubId?.clubName || 'Club'}</div>
            <div class="ec-title">${ev.title}</div>
            <div style="font-size:.74rem;color:var(--v2);margin-bottom:.4rem;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:.3rem">
              👤 ${ev.coordinatorName || 'Club Admin'} · 📞 ${ev.coordinatorPhone || ''}
            </div>
            <div class="ec-meta"><span>📅 ${fDate(ev.date)}</span><span>📍 ${ev.venue}</span></div>
            ${ev.maxParticipants ? `<div class="prog"><div class="prog-fill" style="width:${pct}%"></div></div>
            <div style="font-size:.7rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.7rem">${ev.registeredStudents.length}/${ev.maxParticipants} students</div>` : ''}
            <div class="ec-footer">
              <span></span>
              ${ev.externalLink 
                ? `<a href="${ev.externalLink}" target="_blank" class="btn btn-sm btn-primary" style="text-decoration:none">External Link ↗</a>` 
                : (isReg 
                    ? `<button class="btn btn-sm btn-success" disabled>✅ Registered</button>` 
                    : `<button class="btn btn-sm btn-primary" onclick="quickReg('${ev._id}',this)">Register</button>`)
              }
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>`;
      };

      el.innerHTML = `
        <div class="dash-header" style="margin-bottom:1.5rem"><h1>Discover Events</h1><p>Find your next opportunity.</p></div>
        
        ${recommended.length ? `
        <div class="section-box" style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(124,107,255,.06),rgba(61,230,192,.03));border:1px solid rgba(124,107,255,.2);margin-bottom:2.5rem;overflow:visible">
          <div style="display:inline-block;background:var(--v);color:#fff;font-size:.75rem;font-weight:700;padding:.3rem .8rem;border-radius:100px;margin-bottom:.8rem;box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(124,107,255,.3)">🤖 AI MATCH</div>
          <div class="box-title" style="font-size:1.15rem;margin-bottom:.2rem">Recommended for You</div>
          <p style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.85rem;margin-bottom:1.4rem">Hand-picked based on your department and interests.</p>
          <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fit, minmax(300px, 1fr));gap:1.5rem">
            ${recommended.map(ev => renderCard(ev, true)).join('')}
          </div>
        </div>` : ''}

        <div class="dash-header"><h2>All Upcoming Events</h2><p>${upcoming.length} events available</p></div>
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fit, minmax(300px, 1fr));gap:1.5rem">
          ${upcoming.map(ev => renderCard(ev, false)).join('')}
          ${!upcoming.length ? '<p style="color:var(--tx2);grid-column:1/-1">No upcoming events.</p>' : ''}
        </div>`;
    } catch (err) { el.innerHTML = `<div class="dash-header"><h1>Events</h1></div><p style="color:var(--rd)">${err.message}</p>`; }
  }

  async function quickReg(id, btn, forceReg=false, data=null) {
    if (!Auth.isLoggedIn) { window.location.href='login.html'; return; }
    if (Auth.user.role!=='student') { toast('Only students can register','error'); return; }
    
    // 1. Profile Check: Always ensure student details are present
    const u = Auth.user;
    if (!u.rollNo || !u.department || !u.phone) {
        if (!forceReg) { openRegFormModal(id); return; }
    }

    const events = await API.getEvents();
    const ev = events.find(e => e._id === id);
    if (!ev) return;

    // 2. Fee Check: If not already forcing and there is a fee, ask for payment
    if (!forceReg && ev.participationFee > 0) {
      openPaidRegModal(id, ev);
      return;
    }

    // 3. Final Registration Call
    btn.disabled=true; btn.textContent='…';
    try {
      await API.registerEvent(id, data);
      toast('🎉 Registered! Check your email.','success');
      btn.textContent='✅ Done'; btn.className='btn btn-sm btn-success';
      closeModal();
      await renderEvents();
    } catch (err) {
      toast(err.message,'error'); 
      btn.disabled=false; 
      btn.textContent=ev.participationFee > 0 ? 'Verify Payment & Register' : 'Register';
    }
  }

  function openPaidRegModal(id, ev) {
    document.getElementById('mTitle').textContent = 'Secure Payment Verification';
    document.getElementById('mBody').innerHTML = `
      <div style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:1.5rem">
        <p style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.88rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem">This event requires a participation fee of <strong style="color:var(--v);font-size:1.1rem">₹${ev.participationFee}</strong>.</p>
        
        ${(ev.guests && ev.guests.length > 0) ? `
          <div style="margin-bottom:1.5rem;text-align:left">
            <h4 style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.6rem;text-transform:uppercase">🌟 Special Guests</h4>
            <div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:.5rem">
              ${ev.guests.map(g => `<span class="tag" style="background:rgba(124,107,255,.1);color:var(--v);font-weight:600">${g}</span>`).join('')}
            </div>
          </div>
        ` : ''}

        <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.85rem"><div style="font-size:.68rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">📍 VENUE</div><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:.88rem">${ev.venue}</div></div>
        <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.85rem"><div style="font-size:.68rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">🏢 CLUB</div><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:.88rem">${ev.clubId?.clubName||'Campus Club'}</div></div>
        <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.85rem;grid-column:1/-1">
          <div style="font-size:.68rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">👤 EVENT COORDINATOR</div>
          <div style="font-weight:600;font-size:.88rem">${ev.coordinatorName || 'Club Admin'} · ${ev.coordinatorPhone || ''}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="background:var(--s2);padding:1.5rem;border-radius:12px;margin-bottom:1.5rem;border:1px solid var(--b1)">
          <div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.4rem">Club Admin Payment UPI / Phone</div>
          <div style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:1px">${ev.paymentUpi || 'Not Provided (Contact Club)'}</div>
        </div>

        <div style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:1.5rem">
          <label class="form-label">Upload Payment Screenshot *</label>
          <input type="file" id="payImg" class="form-input" accept="image/*" style="padding:.6rem"/>
          <div style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-top:.5rem">Our AI will scan this image for payment confirmation.</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <button class="btn btn-lg btn-primary" style="width:100%" onclick="submitPaidReg('${id}', this)">Verify Payment & Register</button>
    `;
    document.getElementById('evModal').classList.add('open');
  }

  window.submitPaidReg = async function(id, btn) {
    const fileInput = document.getElementById('payImg');
    if (!fileInput || !fileInput.files.length) { toast('Please upload a screenshot', 'error'); return; }
    
    btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = '🤖 AI Scanning Image...';
    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('paymentProof', fileInput.files[0]);

    // Use the API helper we updated
    quickReg(id, btn, true, formData);
  };

  function openRegFormModal(id) {
    const u = Auth.user;
    document.getElementById('mTitle').textContent = 'Complete Your Profile';
    document.getElementById('mBody').innerHTML = `
      <div style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:1.5rem">
        <p style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.88rem;margin-bottom:1rem">We need a few more details before you can register for events.</p>
        <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Student Roll Number / ID *</label><input class="form-input" id="regRoll" placeholder="e.g. 21BCE001" value="${u.rollNo||''}"/></div>
        <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Department / Course *</label><input class="form-input" id="regDept" placeholder="e.g. Computer Science" value="${u.department||''}"/></div>
        <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Phone Number *</label><input class="form-input" id="regPhone" placeholder="e.g. 9876543210" value="${u.phone||''}"/></div>
      </div>
      <button class="btn btn-lg btn-primary" style="width:100%" onclick="submitRegForm('${id}', this)">Save & Continue</button>
    `;
    document.getElementById('evModal').classList.add('open');
  }

  window.submitRegForm = async function(id, btn) {
    const rollNo = document.getElementById('regRoll').value.trim();
    const department = document.getElementById('regDept').value.trim();
    const phone = document.getElementById('regPhone').value.trim();
    if (!rollNo || !department || !phone) { toast('Please fill all fields', 'error'); return; }
    btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = 'Updating...';
    try {
      await API.updateProfile({ rollNo, department, phone });
      
      // Update local storage and the local variable
      const currentUser = Auth.user; 
      currentUser.rollNo = rollNo; 
      currentUser.department = department; 
      currentUser.phone = phone; 
      Auth.save(currentUser, Auth.token);
      
      // Call quickReg again with forceReg=true to skip profile check, but let it check for fee!
      // Wait, if I call quickReg(id, btn, true), it skips fee check...
      // Let's call quickReg(id, btn, false) instead! Since the profile is now updated, it will pass the first check.
      quickReg(id, btn, false);
    } catch (err) { toast(err.message, 'error'); btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Save & Continue'; }
  };

  function closeModal() { document.getElementById('evModal').classList.remove('open'); }
  document.addEventListener('click', e => { if(e.target.id === 'evModal') closeModal(); });

  async function renderRegistered() {
    const el = document.getElementById('dashMain');
    try {
      const data = await API.getDashboard();
      const regEvs = data.registeredEvents||[];
      el.innerHTML = `
        <div class="dash-header"><h1>My Registrations</h1><p>${regEvs.length} event${regEvs.length!==1?'s':''}</p></div>
        <div class="section-box">
          ${regEvs.map(ev=>`<div class="ev-row">
            <div class="ev-ico">🎯</div>
            <div style="flex:1">
              <div style="font-size:.88rem;font-weight:600">${ev.title}</div>
              <div style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--tx2)">📅 ${fDate(ev.date)} · ⏰ ${ev.time} · 📍 ${ev.venue}</div>
              <div style="margin-top:.3rem">${catTag(ev.category)}</div>
            </div>
            <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:flex-end;gap:.4rem">
              <button class="btn btn-sm btn-success" onclick="showTicket('${ev._id}', '${ev.title.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${ev.date}', '${ev.venue.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">🎟️ Show Ticket</button>
              <button class="btn btn-sm btn-ghost" onclick="cancelReg('${ev._id}',this)" style="font-size: .75rem; color: var(--rd);">Cancel</button>
            </div>
          </div>`).join('')}
          ${!regEvs.length?`<div style="text-align:center;padding:3rem"><div style="font-size:2.5rem;margin-bottom:1rem">📭</div><p style="color:var(--tx2)">No registrations yet.</p><button class="btn btn-md btn-primary" onclick="go('events')" style="margin-top:1rem">Browse Events</button></div>`:''}
        </div>`;
    } catch (err) { document.getElementById('dashMain').innerHTML=`<p style="color:var(--rd)">${err.message}</p>`; }
  }

  async function cancelReg(id, btn) {
    btn.disabled=true;
    try { await API.unregisterEvent(id); toast('Cancelled','info'); go('registered'); }
    catch (err) { toast(err.message,'error'); btn.disabled=false; }
  }

  window.showTicket = function(eventId, title, date, venue) {
    document.getElementById('mTitle').textContent = '🎟️ Event Ticket';
    document.getElementById('mBody').innerHTML = `
      <div style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:1.5rem">
        <h3 style="margin-bottom:.5rem">${title}</h3>
        <p style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.88rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem">📅 ${fDate(date)} · 📍 ${venue}</p>
        <div id="qrcodeBox" style="background:#fff;padding:1rem;border-radius:12px;display:inline-block;margin-bottom:1rem"></div>
        <p style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.8rem">Show this QR code at the entrance to check in.</p>
      </div>
    `;
    
    // Generate secure QR payload
    const payload = JSON.stringify({ eventId: eventId, studentId: Auth.user._id });
    new QRCode(document.getElementById('qrcodeBox'), {
      text: payload,
      width: 200,
      height: 200,
      colorDark : "#000000",
      colorLight : "#ffffff",
      correctLevel : QRCode.CorrectLevel.H
    });

    document.getElementById('evModal').classList.add('open');
  };

  function renderProfile() {
    document.getElementById('dashMain').innerHTML = `
      <div class="dash-header"><h1>Profile Settings</h1></div>
      <div class="section-box">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:1.4rem;padding-bottom:1.8rem;margin-bottom:1.8rem;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1)">
          <div class="avatar av-xl">${user.name[0].toUpperCase()}</div>
          <div><h2 style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:1.3rem;font-weight:800">${user.name}</h2><p style="color:var(--tx2)">${user.email}</p><div style="margin-top:.4rem"><span class="tag tag-v">🎓 Student</span></div></div>
        </div>
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:1.2rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem">
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Full Name</label><input class="form-input" id="pName" value="${user.name}"/></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Email</label><input class="form-input" value="${user.email}" disabled style="opacity:.5"/></div>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-bottom:1.5rem">
          <label class="form-label" style="display:block;margin-bottom:.7rem">Interests</label>
          <div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:.4rem" id="intChips">
            ${['Technical','Cultural','Sports','Hackathons','Workshops','AI','Arts','Entrepreneurship','Coding'].map(i=>`
              <button class="int-chip-sm ${(user.interests||[]).includes(i)?'sel':''}" onclick="this.classList.toggle('sel')" data-v="${i}">${i}</button>`).join('')}
          </div>
        </div>
        <button class="btn btn-md btn-primary" onclick="saveProfile()">Save Changes</button>
      </div>`;
  }

  async function saveProfile() {
    const name = document.getElementById('pName').value.trim();
    const interests = [...document.querySelectorAll('.int-chip-sm.sel')].map(el=>el.dataset.v);
    try {
      await Promise.all([
        API.updateProfile({ name }),
        API.updateInterests({ interests }),
      ]);
      user.name=name; user.interests=interests;
      Auth.save(user, Auth.token);
      toast('Profile saved!','success');
      buildSidebar();
    } catch (err) { toast(err.message,'error'); }
  }

  async function renderFollowedFeed() {
    const feedEl = document.getElementById('followedFeed');
    try {
      const updates = await API.getAnnouncements(); // This uses the feed endpoint check clubController
      if (!updates || !updates.length) return;
      
      feedEl.innerHTML = `
        <div class="section-box" style="margin-top:0">
          <div class="box-title">🚀 Updates from Followed Clubs</div>
          ${updates.map(up => `
            <div class="notif pk" style="display:flex;gap:1rem;align-items:flex-start">
              <div style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:8px;background:var(--s1);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-shrink:0">📣</div>
              <div>
                <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:0.85rem;margin-bottom:0.2rem">${up.title} <span style="font-weight:400;color:var(--tx2);font-size:0.75rem">· ${up.clubId?.clubName}</span></div>
                <div style="color:var(--tx2);line-height:1.4">${up.content}</div>
                <div style="font-size:0.7rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-top:0.4rem">${fDate(up.createdAt)}</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          `).join('')}
        </div>
      `;
    } catch (e) { console.error('Feed error:', e); }
  }

  buildSidebar(); go('overview');
</script>
</body>
</html>


// FILE: pages\events.html
// ========================================
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en" data-theme="dark">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8"/><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1.0"/>
  <title>Events — CampusConnect</title>
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/style.css"/>
  <style>
    .events-grid{display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr);gap:1.4rem}
    @media(max-width:900px){.events-grid{grid-template-columns:repeat(2,1fr)}}
    @media(max-width:580px){.events-grid{grid-template-columns:1fr}}
  </style>
</head>
<body>
<nav class="navbar" id="mainNav"></nav>
<div class="page-wrap">
  <div class="page-hero">
    <div class="container">
      <span class="section-label">✦ Discover</span>
      <h1>Campus Events</h1>
      <p style="color:var(--tx2);margin-top:.4rem">Browse hackathons, workshops, cultural events and more.</p>
    </div>
  </div>
  <div class="container" style="padding:2rem 0 4rem">
    <div class="filters">
      <div class="search-box"><span class="s-ico">🔍</span><input type="text" id="searchInput" placeholder="Search events…"/></div>
      <div class="cat-pills" id="catPills"></div>
      <select class="form-select" id="sortSel" style="width:auto">
        <option value="date">Soonest First</option>
        <option value="popular">Most Popular</option>
        <option value="free">Free First</option>
      </select>
    </div>
    <div id="resultsInfo" style="margin-bottom:1.2rem;color:var(--tx2);font-size:.85rem"></div>
    <div class="events-grid" id="eventsGrid"></div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Event Detail Modal -->
<div class="modal-overlay" id="evModal">
  <div class="modal" style="max-width:580px">
    <div class="modal-header"><div class="modal-title" id="mTitle"></div><button class="modal-close" onclick="closeModal()">✕</button></div>
    <div id="mBody"></div>
  </div>
</div>

<footer id="mainFooter"></footer>
<script src="../js/app.js"></script>
<script>
  buildNav('events');

  const CATS = ['All','Technical','Cultural','Sports','Hackathons','Workshops','Entrepreneurship','Arts'];
  let allEvents = [];
  let activeCat = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get('cat') || 'All';
  let search = '', sort = 'date';

  // Build pills
  const pillsEl = document.getElementById('catPills');
  CATS.forEach(c => {
    const b = document.createElement('button');
    b.className = 'cat-pill'+(c===activeCat?' active':'');
    b.textContent = c;
    b.onclick = () => { activeCat=c; document.querySelectorAll('.cat-pill').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('active')); b.classList.add('active'); render(); };
    pillsEl.appendChild(b);
  });

  document.getElementById('searchInput').addEventListener('input', e => { search=e.target.value.toLowerCase(); render(); });
  document.getElementById('sortSel').addEventListener('change', e => { sort=e.target.value; render(); });

  async function loadEvents() {
    const grid = document.getElementById('eventsGrid');
    loading(grid);
    try {
      allEvents = await API.getEvents();
      render();
    } catch {
      grid.innerHTML = `<div style="grid-column:1/-1;text-align:center;padding:4rem">
        <p style="color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.5rem">⚠️ Could not connect to backend.</p>
        <p style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.82rem">Make sure your Node.js server is running on port 5000.</p>
      </div>`;
    }
  }

  function getFiltered() {
    let list = [...allEvents];
    if (activeCat!=='All') list = list.filter(e=>e.category===activeCat);
    if (search) list = list.filter(e=>e.title.toLowerCase().includes(search)||(e.clubId?.clubName||'').toLowerCase().includes(search));
    if (sort==='popular') list.sort((a,b)=>b.registeredStudents.length-a.registeredStudents.length);
    else if (sort==='free') list.sort((a,b)=>a.participationFee-b.participationFee);
    else list.sort((a,b)=>new Date(a.date)-new Date(b.date));
    return list;
  }

  function isRegistered(ev) {
    const u = Auth.user;
    if (!u) return false;
    return ev.registeredStudents.some(s => (s._id||s)===u._id);
  }

  function render() {
    const list = getFiltered();
    const grid = document.getElementById('eventsGrid');
    document.getElementById('resultsInfo').textContent = `${list.length} event${list.length!==1?'s':''} found`;
    if (!list.length) { empty(grid,'No events found. Try a different filter.'); return; }

    grid.innerHTML = list.map(ev => {
      const reg = isRegistered(ev);
      const isFull = ev.maxParticipants && ev.registeredStudents.length >= ev.maxParticipants;
      const pct = ev.maxParticipants ? Math.round((ev.registeredStudents.length/ev.maxParticipants)*100) : 0;
      
      let btnText = reg ? '✅ Registered' : (isFull ? 'Join Waitlist' : 'Register');
      let btnClass = reg ? 'btn-success' : (isFull ? 'btn-ghost' : 'btn-primary');
      let isActionReg = reg;
      if (isFull && !reg && ev.waitlistStudents && ev.waitlistStudents.includes(Auth.user?._id)) {
        btnText = '⏳ Waitlisted';
        btnClass = 'btn-success';
        isActionReg = true;
      }

      return `<div class="event-card" onclick="openModal('${ev._id}')">
        <div class="ec-img" style="background:var(--s2);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:3.5rem"> 
          ${(() => {
            const icons = { 'Technical': '💻', 'Cultural': '🎭', 'Sports': '🏆', 'Hackathons': '🚀', 'Workshops': '🛠️', 'Entrepreneurship': '💡', 'Arts': '🎨' };
            return icons[ev.category] || '🎯';
          })()}
          <div style="position:absolute;top:.8rem;right:.8rem"><span class="tag ${ev.participationFee===0?'tag-gn':'tag-am'}">${ev.participationFee===0?'Free':'₹'+ev.participationFee}</span></div>
        </div>
        <div class="ec-body">
          <div class="ec-club">🏢 ${ev.clubId?.clubName||'Campus Club'}</div>
          <div class="ec-title">${ev.title}</div>
          <div style="font-size:.74rem;color:var(--v2);margin-bottom:.4rem;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:.3rem">
            👤 ${ev.coordinatorName || 'Club Admin'} · 📞 ${ev.coordinatorPhone || ''}
          </div>
          <div class="ec-meta">
            <span>📅 ${fDate(ev.date)} · ${ev.time}</span>
            <span>📍 ${ev.venue}</span>
            <span>⏰ Deadline: ${fDate(ev.registrationDeadline)}</span>
          </div>
          ${ev.maxParticipants?`<div class="prog"><div class="prog-fill" style="width:${pct}%"></div></div>
          <div style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.7rem">${ev.registeredStudents.length}/${ev.maxParticipants} (${Math.min(pct, 100)}%) ${isFull ? '— <strong>Seats Full</strong>' : ''}</div>`:''}
          <div class="ec-footer">
            <span></span>
            ${ev.externalLink ? 
               `<a class="btn btn-sm btn-primary" style="text-decoration:none" href="${ev.externalLink}" target="_blank" onclick="event.stopPropagation()">Register Externally ↗</a>` :
               `<button class="btn btn-sm ${btnClass}" onclick="event.stopPropagation();toggleReg('${ev._id}',this,${isActionReg})">
                 ${btnText}
               </button>`
            }
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
  }

  async function toggleReg(id, btn, wasReg, forceReg=false, data=null) {
    if (!Auth.isLoggedIn) { window.location.href='login.html'; return; }
    if (Auth.user.role!=='student') { toast('Only students can register','error'); return; }
    
    // If we're not registered and not forcing registration directly, ask for details first!
    if (!wasReg && !forceReg) {
      openRegFormModal(id);
      return;
    }

    btn.disabled=true; btn.textContent='…';
    try {
      if (wasReg) {
        const res = await API.unregisterEvent(id);
        toast(res.message || 'Unregistered', 'info');
      } else {
        const res = await API.registerEvent(id, data);
        const msg = res.message || 'Registered! Check your email.';
        toast(msg, msg.toLowerCase().includes('waitlist') ? 'info' : 'success');
      }
      await loadEvents(); // refresh
      // Also close the modal if it's open and displaying the registration form
      if(!wasReg) closeModal();
    } catch (err) {
      toast(err.message,'error');
      btn.disabled=false;
      btn.textContent=wasReg?'✅ Registered':'Confirm Registration';
    }
  }

  function openRegFormModal(id) {
    const u = Auth.user;
    const ev = allEvents.find(e => e._id === id);
    if (!ev) return;

    document.getElementById('mTitle').textContent = 'Registration Details';
    
    let paymentUI = '';
    if (ev.participationFee > 0) {
      paymentUI = `
        <div style="margin-top:1.5rem;padding:1.2rem;background:rgba(255,193,7,0.05);border:1px dashed var(--am);border-radius:var(--r)">
          <h4 style="color:var(--am);margin-bottom:.5rem;font-size:.9rem">💰 Payment Required</h4>
          <p style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:1rem">This is a paid event. Please pay <strong>₹${ev.participationFee}</strong> to the UPI ID below and upload a screenshot of the transaction.</p>
          
          <div style="background:var(--s2);padding:.8rem;border-radius:8px;text-align:center;margin-bottom:1.2rem">
            <div style="font-size:.65rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">UPI ID</div>
            <div style="font-weight:700;letter-spacing:1px;color:var(--tx1)">${ev.paymentUpi || 'campusconnect@upi'}</div>
          </div>

          <div class="form-group">
            <label class="form-label">Payment Screenshot *</label>
            <input type="file" class="form-input" id="regPayment" accept="image/*" style="padding:.5rem"/>
            <small style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.7rem">Make sure the transaction ID and amount are visible.</small>
          </div>
        </div>
      `;
    }

    document.getElementById('mBody').innerHTML = `
      <div style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:1.5rem">
        <div style="display:flex;gap:1.5rem;margin-bottom:1.2rem;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1);padding-bottom:1rem">
          <div><div style="font-size:.65rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">📅 DATE</div><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:.85rem">${fDate(ev.date)}</div></div>
          <div><div style="font-size:.65rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">📍 VENUE</div><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:.85rem">${ev.venue}</div></div>
        </div>
        ${(ev.guests && ev.guests.length > 0) ? `
          <div style="margin-bottom:1.5rem">
            <h4 style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.6rem;text-transform:uppercase">🌟 Special Guests</h4>
            <div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:.5rem">
              ${ev.guests.map(g => `<span class="tag" style="background:rgba(124,107,255,.1);color:var(--v);font-weight:600">${g}</span>`).join('')}
            </div>
          </div>
        ` : ''}
        <p style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.88rem;margin-bottom:1.2rem">Complete your profile and payment (if applicable) to join.</p>
        
        <div class="form-group">
          <label class="form-label">Student Roll Number / ID *</label>
          <input class="form-input" id="regRoll" placeholder="e.g. 21BCE001" value="${u.rollNo||''}"/>
        </div>
        <div class="form-group">
          <label class="form-label">Department / Course *</label>
          <input class="form-input" id="regDept" placeholder="e.g. Computer Science" value="${u.department||''}"/>
        </div>
        <div class="form-group">
          <label class="form-label">Phone Number *</label>
          <input class="form-input" id="regPhone" placeholder="e.g. 9876543210" value="${u.phone||''}"/>
        </div>

        ${paymentUI}

        <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:12px;padding:1.2rem;margin-top:1.5rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem">
          <h4 style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.8rem;text-transform:uppercase">Contact Organizer</h4>
          <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:.6rem;font-size:.85rem">
            ${ev.clubId?.contactEmail ? `<div><span style="color:var(--tx2)">📧 Email:</span> <a href="mailto:${ev.clubId.contactEmail}" style="color:var(--v);text-decoration:none;font-weight:600">${ev.clubId.contactEmail}</a></div>` : ''}
            ${ev.clubId?.contactPhone ? `<div><span style="color:var(--tx2)">📞 Phone:</span> <span style="font-weight:600">${ev.clubId.contactPhone}</span></div>` : ''}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <button class="btn btn-lg btn-primary" style="width:100%" onclick="submitRegForm('${id}', this)">
        Complete & Register
      </button>
    `;
    document.getElementById('evModal').classList.add('open');
  }

  window.submitRegForm = async function(id, btn) {
    const ev = allEvents.find(e => e._id === id);
    const rollNo = document.getElementById('regRoll').value.trim();
    const department = document.getElementById('regDept').value.trim();
    const phone = document.getElementById('regPhone').value.trim();
    
    if (!rollNo || !department || !phone) { toast('Please fill all profile fields', 'error'); return; }
    
    const formData = new FormData();
    if (ev.participationFee > 0) {
      const fileInput = document.getElementById('regPayment');
      if (!fileInput || !fileInput.files[0]) {
        toast('Please upload a payment screenshot for this paid event', 'error');
        return;
      }
      formData.append('paymentProof', fileInput.files[0]);
    }
    
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.textContent = 'Processing...';
    
    try {
      // 1. Update Profile (if changed)
      if (rollNo !== Auth.user.rollNo || department !== Auth.user.department || phone !== Auth.user.phone) {
        await API.updateProfile({ rollNo, department, phone });
        Auth.user.rollNo = rollNo; Auth.user.department = department; Auth.user.phone = phone;
        Auth.save(Auth.user, Auth.token);
      }
      
      // 2. Proceed to register with potential file data
      toggleReg(id, btn, false, true, formData);
    } catch (err) {
      toast(err.message, 'error');
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = 'Complete & Register';
    }
  };

  async function openModal(id) {
    const ev = allEvents.find(e=>e._id===id);
    if (!ev) return;
    const reg = isRegistered(ev);
    const isFull = ev.maxParticipants && ev.registeredStudents.length >= ev.maxParticipants;
    const pct = ev.maxParticipants ? Math.round((ev.registeredStudents.length/ev.maxParticipants)*100) : 0;
    
    let btnText = reg ? '✅ Registered' : (isFull ? 'Join Waitlist' : 'Register');
    let btnClass = reg ? 'btn-success' : (isFull ? 'btn-ghost' : 'btn-primary');
    let isActionReg = reg;
    if (isFull && !reg && ev.waitlistStudents && ev.waitlistStudents.includes(Auth.user?._id)) {
      btnText = '⏳ Waitlisted';
      btnClass = 'btn-success';
      isActionReg = true;
    }
    document.getElementById('mTitle').textContent = ev.title;
    document.getElementById('mBody').innerHTML = `
      <div class="modal-body">
      <div style="width:100%;height:200px;background:var(--s2);border-radius:12px;margin-bottom:1.5rem;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:4.5rem">
        ${(() => {
          const icons = { 'Technical': '💻', 'Cultural': '🎭', 'Sports': '🏆', 'Hackathons': '🚀', 'Workshops': '🛠️', 'Entrepreneurship': '💡', 'Arts': '🎨' };
          return icons[ev.category] || '🎯';
        })()}
      </div>
      <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:.8rem;margin-bottom:1.4rem">${catTag(ev.category)}<span class="tag ${ev.participationFee===0?'tag-gn':'tag-am'}">${ev.participationFee===0?'Free':'₹'+ev.participationFee}</span></div>
      
      <p style="color:var(--tx2);font-size:.88rem;line-height:1.7;margin-bottom:1.5rem">${ev.description}</p>
      
      ${(ev.guests && ev.guests.length > 0) ? `
        <div style="margin-bottom:1.5rem">
          <h4 style="font-family:'Syne',sans-serif;font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.6rem;text-transform:uppercase">🌟 Special Guests</h4>
          <div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:.5rem">
            ${ev.guests.map(g => `<span class="tag" style="background:rgba(124,107,255,.1);color:var(--v);font-weight:600">${g}</span>`).join('')}
          </div>
        </div>
      ` : ''}

      <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:.7rem;margin-bottom:1.4rem">
        <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.85rem"><div style="font-size:.68rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">📅 DATE</div><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:.88rem">${fDate(ev.date)}</div></div>
        <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.85rem"><div style="font-size:.68rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">⏰ TIME</div><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:.88rem">${ev.time}</div></div>
        <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.85rem"><div style="font-size:.68rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">📍 VENUE</div><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:.88rem">${ev.venue}</div></div>
        <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.85rem"><div style="font-size:.68rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">🏢 CLUB</div><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:.88rem">${ev.clubId?.clubName||'Campus Club'}</div></div>
        <div style="background:var(--s2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:10px;padding:.85rem;grid-column:1/-1">
          <div style="font-size:.68rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:.2rem">👤 EVENT COORDINATOR</div>
          <div style="font-weight:600;font-size:.88rem">${ev.coordinatorName || 'Club Admin'} · ${ev.coordinatorPhone || ''}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      ${ev.maxParticipants?`<div class="prog" style="margin-bottom:.4rem"><div class="prog-fill" style="width:${pct}%"></div></div><div style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--tx2);margin-bottom:1.4rem">${ev.registeredStudents.length}/${ev.maxParticipants} spots filled ${isFull ? '(Seats Full)' : ''}</div>`:''}
      ${ev.externalLink ? 
        `<a class="btn btn-lg btn-primary" style="width:100%;text-decoration:none;display:block;box-sizing:border-box" target="_blank" href="${ev.externalLink}">Register on External Website ↗</a>` :
        `<button class="btn btn-lg ${btnClass}" style="width:100%" id="mRegBtn" onclick="toggleReg('${id}',this,${isActionReg})">
          ${isActionReg ? (btnText === '⏳ Waitlisted' ? '⏳ Waitlisted — Cancel?' : '✅ Registered — Cancel?') : (isFull ? 'Seats Full — Join Waitlist' : 'Register Now')}
        </button>`
      }`;
    document.getElementById('evModal').classList.add('open');
  }

  function closeModal() { document.getElementById('evModal').classList.remove('open'); }
  document.getElementById('evModal').addEventListener('click', e => { if(e.target===e.currentTarget) closeModal(); });

  loadEvents();
</script>
</body>
</html>


// FILE: pages\login.html
// ========================================
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en" data-theme="dark">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8"/><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1.0"/>
  <title>Login — CampusConnect</title>
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/style.css"/>
  <style>
    .auth-wrap{min-height:100vh;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;padding:6rem 1.5rem 3rem;position:relative;overflow:hidden}
    .orb{position:absolute;border-radius:50%;filter:blur(72px);pointer-events:none}
    .o1{width:400px;height:400px;background:rgba(124,107,255,.15);top:-100px;left:-100px;animation:float 8s ease-in-out infinite}

      <button class="btn btn-sm btn-ghost" onclick="demoLogin('clubAdmin')">🏢 Club Admin</button>
      <button class="btn btn-sm btn-ghost" onclick="demoLogin('superAdmin')">👑 Admin</button>
