<script src="../js/app.js"></script>
<script>
  buildNav('');
  if (Auth.isLoggedIn) { const u=Auth.user; window.location.href=u.role==='clubAdmin'?'club-dashboard.html':u.role==='superAdmin'?'admin.html':'dashboard.html'; }

  let role = 'student';
  function setRole(r) {
    role = r;
    document.querySelectorAll('.r-tab').forEach(t=>t.classList.remove('active'));
    document.getElementById('tab-'+r).classList.add('active');
  }

  async function handleLogin() {
    const email = document.getElementById('email').value.trim();
    const password = document.getElementById('password').value;
    if (!email||!password) { toast('Please fill in all fields','error'); return; }
    const btn = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
    btn.textContent='Signing in…'; btn.disabled=true;
    try {
      const data = await API.login({ email, password });
      Auth.save(data.user, data.token);
      toast('Login successful! Redirecting…','success');
      setTimeout(() => {
        const r = data.user.role;
        window.location.href = r==='clubAdmin'?'club-dashboard.html':r==='superAdmin'?'admin.html':'dashboard.html';
      }, 700);
    } catch (err) {
      toast(err.message||'Login failed','error');
      btn.textContent='Sign In'; btn.disabled=false;
    }
  }

  // Demo: creates temp accounts in backend, or uses pre-seeded ones
  async function demoLogin(r) {
    const demos = {
      student:    { name:'Demo Student',    email:'demo.student@college.edu',    password:'demo1234', role:'student',    interests:['Technical','Hackathons','AI'] },
      clubAdmin:  { name:'Demo Club Admin', email:'demo.clubadmin@college.edu',  password:'demo1234', role:'clubAdmin'  },
      superAdmin: { name:'Demo Super Admin',email:'demo.superadmin@college.edu', password:'demo1234', role:'superAdmin' },
    };
    const d = demos[r];
    try {
      // Try login first
      const data = await API.login({ email: d.email, password: d.password });
      Auth.save(data.user, data.token);
    } catch {
      // If not exists, register
      try {
        const data = await API.register(d);
        Auth.save(data.user, data.token);
      } catch (err) {
        toast(err.message,'error'); return;
      }
    }
    toast(`Logged in as Demo ${r}!`,'success');
    setTimeout(() => { window.location.href = r==='clubAdmin'?'club-dashboard.html':r==='superAdmin'?'admin.html':'dashboard.html'; }, 700);
  }
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script src="../js/app.js"></script>
<script>
  buildNav('');
  if (Auth.isLoggedIn) window.location.href = 'dashboard.html';

  let role = 'student';
  let interests = [];

  const urlRole = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get('role');
  if (urlRole === 'clubAdmin') setTimeout(() => setRole('clubAdmin'), 80);

  function setRole(r) {
    role = r;
    document.querySelectorAll('.r-tab').forEach(t=>t.classList.remove('active'));
    document.getElementById('tab-'+r).classList.add('active');
    document.getElementById('interestSection').style.display = r==='student'?'':'none';
    document.getElementById('clubSection').style.display = r==='clubAdmin'?'flex':'none';
  }

  function toggleInt(el, v) {
    el.classList.toggle('sel');
    interests = el.classList.contains('sel') ? [...interests,v] : interests.filter(i=>i!==v);
  }

  async function handleRegister() {
    const name=document.getElementById('name').value.trim();
    const email=document.getElementById('email').value.trim();
    const password=document.getElementById('password').value;
    if (!name||!email||!password) { toast('Please fill all required fields','error'); return; }
    if (password.length<6) { toast('Password must be at least 6 characters','error'); return; }

    const btn = document.getElementById('regBtn');
    btn.textContent='Creating account…'; btn.disabled=true;

    try {
      const data = await API.register({ name, email, password, role, interests });
      Auth.save(data.user, data.token);

      // If club admin, also create the club
      if (role==='clubAdmin') {
        const clubName=document.getElementById('clubName').value.trim();
        const category=document.getElementById('clubCat').value;
        const description=document.getElementById('clubDesc').value.trim();
        const contactEmail=document.getElementById('clubEmail').value.trim();
        const contactPhone=document.getElementById('clubPhone').value.trim();
        if (clubName && category && description) {
          try { await API.createClub({ clubName, category, description, contactEmail, contactPhone }); } catch {}
        }
      }

      toast('🎉 Account created! Redirecting…','success');
      setTimeout(() => { window.location.href = role==='clubAdmin'?'club-dashboard.html':role==='superAdmin'?'admin.html':'dashboard.html'; }, 800);
    } catch (err) {
      toast(err.message||'Registration failed','error');
      btn.textContent='Create Account'; btn.disabled=false;
    }
  }
</script>
</body>
</html>
